2.1.1.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:generic-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:generic-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:generic-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:generic-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:generic-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__GenericDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.3.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:generic-notice/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:generic-notice/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:generic-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:generic-notice/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:generic-notice/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.GenericNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__GenericNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier

2.1.6.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-account-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-account-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-account-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-account-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-account-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrAccountDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrAccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrAccountDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrAccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrAccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrAccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.8.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwres-events-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwres-events-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwres-events-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwres-events-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwres-events-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresEventsDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresEventsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresEventsDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresEventsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresEventsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresEventsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.10.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-config-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-config-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-config-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-config-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-config-debug/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrConfigDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrConfigDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.12.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-virtual-network-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-virtual-network-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-virtual-network-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-virtual-network-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-virtual-network-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrVirtualNetworkInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrVirtualNetworkInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrVirtualNetworkInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrVirtualNetworkInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrVirtualNetworkInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.14.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-security-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-security-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-security-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-security-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-security-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrSecurityInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrSecurityInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrSecurityInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrSecurityInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.16.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-volume-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-volume-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-volume-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-volume-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-volume-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrVolumeInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrVolumeInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrVolumeInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrVolumeInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrVolumeInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrVolumeInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.18.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-info/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrCoreInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrCoreInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrCoreInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrCoreInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrCoreInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.20.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-error/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-error/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-error/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:rwresmgr-core-error/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.RwresmgrCoreError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrCoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__RwresmgrCoreError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrCoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_RwresmgrCoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.22.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:security-group-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:security-group-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:security-group-allocating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:security-group-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:security-group-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.SecurityGroupAllocating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_SecurityGroupAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__SecurityGroupAllocating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_SecurityGroupAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_SecurityGroupAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_SecurityGroupAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.24.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:security-group-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:security-group-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:security-group-releasing/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:security-group-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:security-group-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.SecurityGroupReleasing.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_SecurityGroupReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__SecurityGroupReleasing__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_SecurityGroupReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_SecurityGroupReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_SecurityGroupReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.26.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:connection-point-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:connection-point-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:connection-point-allocating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:connection-point-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:connection-point-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.ConnectionPointAllocating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_ConnectionPointAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__ConnectionPointAllocating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_ConnectionPointAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_ConnectionPointAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier

2.1.28.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:public-ip-creating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:public-ip-creating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:public-ip-creating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:public-ip-creating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:public-ip-creating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.PublicIpCreating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_PublicIpCreating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__PublicIpCreating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.31.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:public-ip-deleted/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:public-ip-deleted/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:public-ip-deleted/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:public-ip-deleted/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:public-ip-deleted/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.PublicIpDeleted.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_PublicIpDeleted_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__PublicIpDeleted__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_PublicIpDeleted_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_PublicIpDeleted_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_PublicIpDeleted_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.33.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:connection-point-released/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:connection-point-released/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:connection-point-released/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:connection-point-released/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:connection-point-released/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.ConnectionPointReleased.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_ConnectionPointReleased_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__ConnectionPointReleased__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.35.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:volume-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:volume-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:volume-allocated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:volume-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:volume-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.VolumeAllocated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_VolumeAllocated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__VolumeAllocated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_VolumeAllocated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.37.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:volume-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:volume-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:volume-releasing/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:volume-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:volume-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.VolumeReleasing.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_VolumeReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__VolumeReleasing__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_VolumeReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwresmgrLog_notif_VolumeReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_VolumeReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.39.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:network-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:network-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:network-allocating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:network-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:network-allocating/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.NetworkAllocating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_NetworkAllocating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__NetworkAllocating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:network-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:network-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:network-releasing/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:network-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:network-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier

2.1.44.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:vdu-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:vdu-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:vdu-allocated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:vdu-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:vdu-allocated/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.VduAllocated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_VduAllocated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__VduAllocated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwresmgrLog_RwresmgrLog_notif_VduAllocated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.46.1.3  container rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwresmgr-log:vdu-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwresmgr-log:vdu-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwresmgr-log:vdu-releasing/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:vdu-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwresmgr-log:vdu-releasing/rwresmgr-log:template_params/rwresmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwresmgr_log.YangNotif.RwresmgrLog.VduReleasing.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwresmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwresmgrLog_VduReleasing_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwresmgrLog__YangNotif__RwresmgrLog__VduReleasing__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
